SLS Exploration Upper Stage passes review

10 Aug 2024, 00:00

WASHINGTON ‚Äî An upgraded upper stage for the Space Launch System rocket has passed a major review, allowing its prime contractor, Boeing, to start producing hardware. Boeing announced Dec. 21 that the Exploration Upper Stage (EUS) of the SLS completed a critical design review with NASA. That review confirmed the design of the EUS, allowing Boeing to proceed with development of the stage, including hardware fabrication. The EUS will be used on the Block 1B variant of SLS, replacing the Interim Cryogenic Propulsion Stage (ICPS) used on the initial Block 1 version of the SLS and based on the Delta 4 upper stage.

Difference Between Heritage And Culture

03 Aug 2024, 00:00

The terms heritage and culture are often used interchangeably, but they have very different meanings. Heritage refers to the transmission of beliefs and values from the past to the present, while culture is the complex system of beliefs, values, behaviour, and material objects shared by a particular group of people. It is important to understand the difference between the two so that we can better appreciate the history and traditions of our society.

Difference Between Conceptual And Operational Variable

23 May 2024, 00:00

A conceptual variable and an operational variable are two distinct concepts that are important to consider when conducting research. Understanding the differences between the two is essential for any researcher to ensure accuracy and validity in their study. A conceptual variable is a concept or idea that can be measured, while an operational variable is the specific way a concept is measured. Definition of Conceptual Variable A conceptual variable is an abstract concept or idea that cannot be observed directly.
